Several reviews mentioned that brand new badger brushes had a foul odor to them that took a while to get rid of. I braced myself as I opened the package, I was prepared for the worst road kill stench known to mankind but this brush had a very slight odor to it that was not particularly objectionable. I took the advice of one of the other reviewers and washed it out in dish washing detergent and then let it soak in a cup with a solution of dish washing detergent and water for about 90 minutes. I never noticed much of an odor during any phase of this process but did notice that the water became somewhat discolored. The brush lost 3 bristles during this process and after using it for a couple of weeks it hasn't lost any more. I have no idea what a $200 silver tip badger brush could do for me but as long this $12.00 beauty continues to perform, I'll have no need to find out.
